#!/bin/zsh

# Build SPEC CPU tools for MacOS X
export PATH=/usr/bin:/bin
echo PATH is $PATH
echo
echo I am
id
echo
echo This system is
uname -a
echo
echo The compiler I will use today is
cc -v
echo

export CPPFLAGS=-no-cpp-precomp
export BZIP2CFLAGS=-O3
export MD5CFLAGS=-O3
export PERLFLAGS='-Doptimize=-O3'

cd tools/src
time ./buildtools

echo
echo Small proof of success:
echo
cd ../..
. ./shrc
specperl -V
echo
touch SUMS.tools
runspec -V
echo
runspec --test
echo
echo Done
